Historical Stress Scenarios\n    20вҶ’\n    21вҶ’Each scenario replays real market data through the full pipeline (features -> regime -> model -> gating -> execution). The goal is to verify the system does not blow up during known extreme events. Historical data is fetched via `scripts/collect_history.py` and stored in the backtest database.\n    22вҶ’\n    23вҶ’### 1.1 March 2020 COVID Crash (BTC -50% in 2 days)\n    24вҶ’\n    25вҶ’**What happened (March 12-13, 2020 -- \"Black Thursday\"):**\n    26вҶ’- BTC fell from ~$7,900 to ~$3,800 in roughly 36 hours (-52%).\n    27вҶ’- BitMEX alone liquidated >$1.6B in 24 hours. Aggregate cross-exchange liquidations exceeded $4B.\n    28вҶ’- Binance order book depth collapsed: top-10 bid levels lost ~80% of volume within minutes.\n    29вҶ’- Bid-ask spreads on BTCUSDT perps widened from ~0.01% to >0.5% at the worst point.\n    30вҶ’- Funding rate went deeply negative (-0.375% on Bitmex in a single 8h period) as shorts dominated.\n    31вҶ’- Volume spiked 5-10x normal -- Binance spot BTC/USDT hit 400K BTC daily volume vs ~50K normal.\n    32вҶ’- Multiple exchanges experienced API outages (BitMEX went down for ~25 minutes, which actually halted the cascade).\n    33вҶ’- The crash was correlated across all asset classes: S&P 500 -9.5% on March 12, NQ followed.\n    34вҶ’\n    35вҶ’**Setup code:**\n    36вҶ’\n    37вҶ’```python\n    38вҶ’# tests/stress/test_historical_covid_crash.py\n    39вҶ’import pytest\n    40вҶ’from datetime import datetime, timezone\n    41вҶ’from ep2_crypto.backtest.walk_forward import WalkForwardEngine\n    42вҶ’from ep2_crypto.backtest.simulator import ExecutionSimulator\n    43вҶ’from ep2_crypto.backtest.metrics import compute_all_metrics\n    44вҶ’from ep2_crypto.stress.scenario_loader import load_historical_scenario\n    45вҶ’\n    46вҶ’class TestCovidCrash:\n    47вҶ’    \"\"\"Replay March 12-13, 2020 through the full system.\"\"\"\n    48вҶ’\n    49вҶ’    @pytest.fixture\n    50вҶ’    def scenario_data(self):\n    51вҶ’        return load_historical_scenario(\n    52вҶ’            start=datetime(2020, 3, 10, tzinfo=timezone.utc),\n    53вҶ’            end=datetime(2020, 3, 15, tzinfo=timezone.utc),\n    54вҶ’            symbol=\"BTC/USDT:USDT\",\n    55вҶ’            include_orderbook=True,\n    56вҶ’            include_liquidations=True,\n    57вҶ’            include_funding=True,\n    58вҶ’            # Inject realistic conditions\n    59вҶ’            spread_multiplier=10.0,    # spreads widened ~10x\n    60вҶ’            depth_multiplier=0.2,      # book depth dropped to 20%\n    61вҶ’            slippage_multiplier=5.0,   # 5x normal slippage\n    62вҶ’        )\n    63вҶ’\n    64вҶ’    def test_max_drawdown_bounded(self, scenario_data):\n    65вҶ’        \"\"\"System must not exceed 15% drawdown (our max drawdown halt).\"\"\"\n    66вҶ’        result = self._run_backtest(scenario_data)\n    67вҶ’        assert result.max_drawdown_pct < 15.0, (\n    68вҶ’            f\"Max drawdown {result.max_drawdown_pct:.1f}% exceeded 15% limit\"\n    69вҶ’        )\n    70вҶ’\n    71вҶ’    def test_kill_switches_activate(self, scenario_data):\n    72вҶ’        \"\"\"Daily loss limit (3%) and drawdown gate must trigger.\"\"\"\n    73вҶ’        result = self._run_backtest(scenario_data)\n    74вҶ’        assert result.kill_switch_activations > 0, (\n    75вҶ’            \"Kill switches should have activated during COVID crash\"\n    76вҶ’        )\n    77вҶ’        assert result.daily_loss_limit_triggered is True\n    78вҶ’        assert result.drawdown_gate_triggered is True\n    79вҶ’\n    80вҶ’    def test_position_sizing_reduces(self, scenario_data):\n    81вҶ’        \"\"\"Drawdown gate should progressively reduce position size.\"\"\"\n    82вҶ’        result = self._run_backtest(scenario_data)\n    83вҶ’        # After 3% drawdown, position size should start reducing\n    84вҶ’        sizes = result.position_sizes_during_drawdown\n    85вҶ’        assert sizes[-1] < sizes[0] * 0.5, (\n    86вҶ’            \"Position sizing did not reduce by at least 50% during drawdown\"\n    87вҶ’        )\n    88вҶ’\n    89вҶ’    def test_no_trades_during_spread_extreme(self, scenario_data):\n    90вҶ’        \"\"\"System should abstain when spread > 0.1% (10x normal).\"\"\"\n    91вҶ’        result = self._run_backtest(scenario_data)\n    92вҶ’        extreme_spread_trades = [\n    93вҶ’            t for t in result.trades\n    94вҶ’            if t.entry_spread_pct > 0.1\n    95вҶ’        ]\n    96вҶ’        assert len(extreme_spread_trades) == 0, (\n    97вҶ’            f\"{len(extreme_spread_trades)} trades executed during extreme spreads\"\n    98вҶ’        )\n    99вҶ’\n   100вҶ’    def test_pnl_vs_buy_and_hold(self, scenario_data):\n   101вҶ’        \"\"\"System PnL must beat buy-and-hold (which lost -52%).\"\"\"\n   102вҶ’        result = self._run_backtest(scenario_data)\n   103вҶ’        bnh_return = scenario_data.buy_and_hold_return  # ~-52%\n   104вҶ’        assert result.total_return_pct > bnh_return, (\n   105вҶ’            f\"System return {result.total_return_pct:.1f}% worse than \"\n   106вҶ’            f\"buy-and-hold {bnh_return:.1f}%\"\n   107вҶ’        )\n   108вҶ’\n   109вҶ’    def _run_backtest(self, scenario_data):\n   110вҶ’        engine = WalkForwardEngine(\n   111вҶ’            train_size=4032, test_size=288, step_size=288, gap=1\n   112вҶ’        )\n   113вҶ’        simulator = ExecutionSimulator(\n   114вҶ’            slippage_model=\"sqrt_impact\",\n   115вҶ’            maker_fee_bps=2.0,\n   116вҶ’            taker_fee_bps=4.0,\n   117вҶ’            latency_ms=200,\n   118вҶ’        )\n   119вҶ’        return engine.run(scenario_data, simulator)\n   120вҶ’```\n   121вҶ’\n   122вҶ’**Pass/fail criteria:**\n   123вҶ’| Criterion | Pass | Fail |\n   124вҶ’|-----------|------|------|\n   125вҶ’| Max drawdown | < 15% | >= 15% |\n   126вҶ’| Kill switch activation | Triggered within first 5% drawdown | Never triggered |\n   127вҶ’| Position sizing | Reduced by >= 50% during drawdown | No reduction |\n   128вҶ’| Trades during extreme spread | 0 | Any |\n   129вҶ’| System return vs buy-and-hold | Better than -52% | Worse |\n   130вҶ’\n   131вҶ’**Hardening if test fails:**\n   132вҶ’- If drawdown exceeds 15%: Tighten daily loss limit from 3% to 2%. Add volatility-adaptive position sizing that cuts to zero when 5-min realized vol exceeds 200% annualized.\n   133вҶ’- If kill switch does not activate: Review kill switch thresholds in `config.py`. Ensure the drawdown gate monitors mark-to-market PnL, not just realized PnL.\n   134вҶ’- If trades happen during extreme spreads: Add a spread filter to the confidence gating pipeline: `if current_spread > 5 * rolling_median_spread: abstain`.\n   135вҶ’\n   136вҶ’---\n   137вҶ’\n   138вҶ’### 1.2 May 2021 China Mining Ban Crash (-30% in hours)\n   139вҶ’\n   140вҶ’**What happened (May 19, 2021 -- \"Black Wednesday\"):**\n   141вҶ’- BTC dropped from ~$43K to ~$30K in roughly 8 hours (-30%).\n   142вҶ’- Triggered by China announcing a ban on crypto mining + financial institutions barred from crypto services.\n   143вҶ’- Aggregate liquidations exceeded $8B in 24 hours -- the largest single-day liquidation event in crypto history.\n   144вҶ’- Funding rate had been elevated at +0.05% to +0.10% for days prior (excessive long positioning).\n   145вҶ’- Open interest was at all-time highs (~$27B across exchanges).\n   146вҶ’- The cascade exhibited classic self-exciting dynamics: each wave of liquidations triggered the next.\n   147вҶ’- Order book depth on Binance dropped by ~70% within the first hour.\n   148вҶ’- NQ was relatively flat -- this was a crypto-specific event, meaning cross-market signals would have been misleading.\n   149вҶ’\n   150вҶ’**Setup code:**\n   151вҶ’\n   152вҶ’```python\n   153вҶ’class TestChinaBanCrash:\n   154вҶ’    \"\"\"Replay May 19, 2021 through the full system.\"\"\"\n   155вҶ’\n   156вҶ’    @pytest.fixture\n   157вҶ’    def scenario_data(self):\n   158вҶ’        return load_historical_scenario(\n   159вҶ’            start=datetime(2021, 5, 17, tzinfo=timezone.utc),\n   160вҶ’            end=datetime(2021, 5, 22, tzinfo=timezone.utc),\n   161вҶ’            symbol=\"BTC/USDT:USDT\",\n   162вҶ’            include_orderbook=True,\n   163вҶ’            include_liquidations=True,\n   164вҶ’            include_funding=True,\n   165вҶ’            spread_multiplier=8.0,\n   166вҶ’            depth_multiplier=0.3,\n   167вҶ’            slippage_multiplier=4.0,\n   168вҶ’            # Inject pre-crash conditions\n   169вҶ’            pre_crash_funding_rate=0.08,  # elevated\n   170вҶ’            pre_crash_oi_percentile=95,   # near ATH\n   171вҶ’        )\n   172вҶ’\n   173вҶ’    def test_cascade_detector_fires(self, scenario_data):\n   174вҶ’        \"\"\"Liquidation cascade detector must identify the cascade.\"\"\"\n   175вҶ’        result = self._run_backtest(scenario_data)\n   176вҶ’        assert result.cascade_alerts > 0, (\n   177вҶ’            \"Cascade detector did not fire during largest liquidation event ever\"\n   178вҶ’        )\n   179вҶ’        # Must fire within first 30 minutes of the crash starting\n   180вҶ’        first_alert = result.cascade_alert_timestamps[0]\n   181вҶ’        crash_start = datetime(2021, 5, 19, 7, 0, tzinfo=timezone.utc)\n   182вҶ’        assert (first_alert - crash_start).total_seconds() < 1800\n   183вҶ’\n   184вҶ’    def test_funding_rate_warning(self, scenario_data):\n   185вҶ’        \"\"\"System should flag elevated funding as risk before crash.\"\"\"\n   186вҶ’        result = self._run_backtest(scenario_data)\n   187вҶ’        # Funding z-score > 2 should trigger risk reduction\n   188вҶ’        assert result.pre_crash_risk_flags.get(\"funding_extreme\") is True\n   189вҶ’\n   190вҶ’    def test_cross_market_decorrelation_handled(self, scenario_data):\n   191вҶ’        \"\"\"NQ was flat during crypto crash -- system must not assume\n   192вҶ’        correlation holds and trade based on NQ signal.\"\"\"\n   193вҶ’        result = self._run_backtest(scenario_data)\n   194вҶ’        nq_based_trades = [\n   195вҶ’            t for t in result.trades\n   196вҶ’            if t.signal_source == \"macro_event\"\n   197вҶ’            and t.timestamp >= datetime(2021, 5, 19, tzinfo=timezone.utc)\n   198вҶ’        ]\n   199вҶ’        assert len(nq_based_trades) == 0, (\n   200вҶ’            \"System traded on NQ signal during crypto-specific {"parentUuid":"a6a88615-c3d5-4e11-928f-3e181a1dd270","isSidechain":true,"promptId":"037faac4-a90e-48f6-9041-5732c00f999d","agentId":"a1e546999a1783310","type":"user","message":{"role":"user","content":[{"tool_use_id":"toolu_01E2Ktb36NfHS3tqEWJ7jXbb","type":"tool_result","content":"     1вҶ’# Monte Carlo Methods for Validating & Stress-Testing Trading Strategies\n     2вҶ’\n     3вҶ’## Context: 5-Minute BTC Prediction System\n     4вҶ’\n     5вҶ’This document provides 12 Monte Carlo validation methods with full Python implementations,\n     6вҶ’interpretation guidelines, and sample outputs calibrated for a 55% accuracy 5-minute crypto\n     7вҶ’strategy executing ~105,000 trades/year (one trade per 5-min bar, 365 days).\n     8вҶ’\n     9вҶ’**Baseline strategy assumptions throughout this document:**\n    10вҶ’- Win rate: 55%\n    11вҶ’- Average win: 0.15% (7.5 bps after fees)\n    12вҶ’- Average loss: -0.12% (6 bps after fees)\n    13вҶ’- ~288 trades/day, ~105,120 trades/year\n    14вҶ’- Fees: 0.02% per side (maker on Binance)\n    15вҶ’- Initial capital: $100,000\n    16вҶ’\n    17вҶ’---\n    18вҶ’\n    19вҶ’## 1. Bootstrap Resampling of Trades\n    20вҶ’\n    21вҶ’### What It Does\n    22вҶ’\n    23вҶ’Resamples historical trades **with replacement** to create thousands of alternative equity\n    24вҶ’curves from the same trade population. Answers: \"Given these trades, what range of outcomes\n    25вҶ’was possible?\"\n    26вҶ’\n    27вҶ’### Why Block Bootstrap\n    28вҶ’\n    29вҶ’Individual trade resampling assumes independence. In reality, crypto trades cluster:\n    30вҶ’a winning trade during a breakout is likely followed by more winners. Block bootstrap\n    31вҶ’preserves this autocorrelation by resampling contiguous blocks of trades.\n    32вҶ’\n    33вҶ’**Block length selection:** For 5-min trades, use blocks of 12-288 trades (1 hour to 1 day).\n    34вҶ’The optimal block length can be estimated using the method of Politis and White (2004),\n    35вҶ’implemented in the `arch` Python package.\n    36вҶ’\n    37вҶ’### Full Implementation\n    38вҶ’\n    39вҶ’```python\n    40вҶ’import numpy as np\n    41вҶ’from dataclasses import dataclass\n    42вҶ’from typing import Optional\n    43вҶ’\n    44вҶ’\n    45вҶ’@dataclass\n    46вҶ’class BootstrapResult:\n    47вҶ’    \"\"\"Results from bootstrap resampling of trades.\"\"\"\n    48вҶ’    equity_curves: np.ndarray        # (n_simulations, n_trades)\n    49вҶ’    sharpe_ratios: np.ndarray        # (n_simulations,)\n    50вҶ’    max_drawdowns: np.ndarray        # (n_simulations,)\n    51вҶ’    cagr_values: np.ndarray          # (n_simulations,)\n    52вҶ’    final_equity: np.ndarray         # (n_simulations,)\n    53вҶ’\n    54вҶ’\n    55вҶ’def max_drawdown(equity_curve: np.ndarray) -> float:\n    56вҶ’    \"\"\"Compute maximum drawdown from an equity curve.\"\"\"\n    57вҶ’    peak = np.maximum.accumulate(equity_curve)\n    58вҶ’    drawdown = (equity_curve - peak) / peak\n    59вҶ’    return float(drawdown.min())\n    60вҶ’\n    61вҶ’\n    62вҶ’def compute_sharpe(returns: np.ndarray, periods_per_year: int = 105_120) -> float:\n    63вҶ’    \"\"\"Annualized Sharpe ratio for high-frequency returns.\"\"\"\n    64вҶ’    if returns.std() == 0:\n    65вҶ’        return 0.0\n    66вҶ’    return float(returns.mean() / returns.std() * np.sqrt(periods_per_year))\n    67вҶ’\n    68вҶ’\n    69вҶ’def compute_cagr(\n    70вҶ’    final_value: float,\n    71вҶ’    initial_value: float,\n    72вҶ’    n_periods: int,\n    73вҶ’    periods_per_year: int = 105_120,\n    74вҶ’) -> float:\n    75вҶ’    \"\"\"Annualized compound growth rate.\"\"\"\n    76вҶ’    if initial_value <= 0 or final_value <= 0:\n    77вҶ’        return -1.0\n    78вҶ’    years = n_periods / periods_per_year\n    79вҶ’    if years <= 0:\n    80вҶ’        return 0.0\n    81вҶ’    return float((final_value / initial_value) ** (1.0 / years) - 1.0)\n    82вҶ’\n    83вҶ’\n    84вҶ’def estimate_optimal_block_length(returns: np.ndarray) -> int:\n    85вҶ’    \"\"\"\n    86вҶ’    Estimate optimal block length using Politis-White (2004) method.\n    87вҶ’    Falls back to sqrt(n) heuristic if arch is not available.\n    88вҶ’    \"\"\"\n    89вҶ’    try:\n    90вҶ’        from arch.bootstrap import optimal_block_length\n    91вҶ’        result = optimal_block_length(returns)\n    92вҶ’        # Use the circular bootstrap estimate\n    93вҶ’        block_len = int(np.ceil(result.iloc[0][\"circular\"]))\n    94вҶ’        return max(1, block_len)\n    95вҶ’    except (ImportError, Exception):\n    96вҶ’        # Heuristic: sqrt(n) capped at 288 (one trading day)\n    97вҶ’        return min(int(np.sqrt(len(returns))), 288)\n    98вҶ’\n    99вҶ’\n   100вҶ’def block_bootstrap_trades("}]},"uuid":"f4f6ab8d-dc21-4d42-8b9d-c209aa7d128a","timestamp":"2026-03-23T13:33:42.096Z","sourceToolAssistantUUID":"a6a88615-c3d5-4e11-928f-3e181a1dd270","userType":"external","entrypoint":"claude-vscode","cwd":"/Users/edgarpocaterra/ep2-crypto","sessionId":"f48c9af0-2e30-4c92-9024-4c84a03f39db","version":"2.1.81","gitBranch":"main","slug":"spicy-gathering-plum"}

This document distills the critical findings that change how we build the system.\n     4вҶ’\n     5вҶ’---\n     6вҶ’\n     7вҶ’## Critical Reality Checks\n     8вҶ’\n     9вҶ’### The Hard Numbers\n    10вҶ’- **Realistic directional accuracy**: 52-56% at 5-min (not 60%+)\n    11вҶ’- **Backtest-to-live degradation**: 50-70% (a Sharpe 2.0 backtest вҶ’ Sharpe 0.6-1.0 live)\n    12вҶ’- **Round-trip costs**: 8-12 bps minimum (taker fee + slippage)\n    13вҶ’- **Minimum gross return per trade**: >15 bps to be profitable after costs\n    14вҶ’- **Alpha half-life in crypto**: 1-6 months for ML-based patterns\n    15вҶ’- **Optimal feature count**: 18-25 (not 200+)\n    16вҶ’- **Monthly infra cost**: $40-100 (minimum viable)\n    17вҶ’\n    18вҶ’### What We Got Wrong in V1 Plan\n    19вҶ’1. **XGBoost вҶ’ LightGBM** вҖ” LightGBM outperforms XGBoost on 5-min crypto by 0.5-1.5%\n    20вҶ’2. **LSTM вҶ’ GRU + TCN** вҖ” GRU trains 20-40% faster, comparable accuracy. TCN is parallelizable and competitive.\n    21вҶ’3. **3 regime-specific models вҶ’ hierarchical ensemble** вҖ” regime detection should be a feature, not model routing (too few samples per regime)\n    22вҶ’4. **On-chain as primary signal вҶ’ on-chain as regime context only** вҖ” academic evidence shows on-chain signals operate at 4h-24h, NOT 5-min\n    23вҶ’5. **Sentiment analysis вҶ’ skip for 5-min** вҖ” too slow. Funding rate is the only useful \"sentiment\" at this timeframe\n    24вҶ’6. **Most TA indicators вҶ’ noise at 5-min** вҖ” MACD, Bollinger, Ichimoku, etc. are useless. Only RSI (with regime filter), short ROC, and ATR survive\n    25вҶ’\n    26вҶ’---\n    27вҶ’\n    28вҶ’## 5 Highest-Impact Changes to the Plan\n    29вҶ’\n    30вҶ’### 1. Core Model: LightGBM + Stacking Ensemble (not XGBoost per-regime)\n    31вҶ’\n    32вҶ’**Old plan**: 3 XGBoost classifiers (one per regime) + 3 GRU regressors\n    33вҶ’**New plan**:\n    34вҶ’- LightGBM (primary classifier) + CatBoost (secondary) + GRU (temporal features)\n    35вҶ’- Stacking meta-learner (logistic regression) combines them\n    36вҶ’- Single model set, not per-regime (regime becomes a feature input)\n    37вҶ’- Add LightGBM quantile regression (5 quantiles) for risk assessment\n    38вҶ’\n    39вҶ’**Why**: Per-regime models fragment already-scarce data. A single ensemble with regime features is more robust. Stacking is the #1 gain after feature engineering (Kaggle consensus + financial ML literature).\n    40вҶ’\n    41вҶ’### 2. Feature Priority: Microstructure First, Everything Else Second\n    42вҶ’\n    43вҶ’**Research consensus**: OFI + OBI + microprice capture 60-80% of achievable 5-min signal.\n    44вҶ’\n    45вҶ’**Tier 1 (must-have, ~15 features)**:\n    46вҶ’- Order book imbalance (weighted, levels 1-3 and 1-5)\n    47вҶ’- Trade flow imbalance (30s and 5min windows)\n    48вҶ’- Bid-ask spread (relative)\n    49вҶ’- Volume delta (1-bar, 5-bar)\n    50вҶ’- Volume rate of change\n    51вҶ’- VWAP deviation (1hr)\n    52вҶ’- Realized vol (5-min, 30-min)\n    53вҶ’- Parkinson vol (30-min)\n    54вҶ’- ROC (1, 3, 6, 12 bars)\n    55вҶ’\n    56вҶ’**Tier 2 (strong additions, ~10 features)**:\n    57вҶ’- Book depth ratio, pressure gradient\n    58вҶ’- Trade arrival rate\n    59вҶ’- EWMA volatility, vol-of-vol\n    60вҶ’- RSI(14), linear regression slope(20)\n    61вҶ’- Price quantile rank(60)\n    62вҶ’\n    63вҶ’**Tier 3 (context, ~5 features)**:\n    64вҶ’- Hour-of-day (sin/cos)\n    65вҶ’- Funding rate\n    66вҶ’- Spread Г— OBI interaction\n    67вҶ’- NQ 5-min returns (lagged 1-3 bars) вҖ” during US hours only\n    68вҶ’- VIX level (regime classifier)\n    69вҶ’\n    70вҶ’### 3. Confidence Gating Pipeline (2-4x Sharpe improvement)\n    71вҶ’\n    72вҶ’The full gating pipeline is the single biggest Sharpe multiplier:\n    73вҶ’\n    74вҶ’```\n    75вҶ’Raw Prediction вҶ’ Calibration (isotonic) вҶ’ Meta-Labeling Gate вҶ’ Ensemble Agreement Check вҶ’ Conformal Prediction Gate вҶ’ Signal Filters (vol, regime, liquidity) вҶ’ Adaptive Threshold вҶ’ Drawdown Gate вҶ’ Position Sizing (quarter-Kelly) вҶ’ EXECUTE or ABSTAIN\n    76вҶ’```\n    77вҶ’\n    78вҶ’Key layers:\n    79вҶ’- **Meta-labeling**: Secondary model predicts \"will THIS trade be profitable?\" вҖ” Lopez de Prado's technique, 50-100% Sharpe improvement\n    80вҶ’- **Conformal prediction**: Prediction set must be singleton {UP} or {DOWN}, not {UP, DOWN}\n    81вҶ’- **Adaptive threshold**: Regime-dependent, updated weekly via rolling Sharpe optimization\n    82вҶ’- **Drawdown gate**: Progressive position reduction 3%вҶ’15%, graduated re-entry\n    83вҶ’\n    84вҶ’### 4. Regime Detection: Hierarchical Ensemble (not just HMM)\n    85вҶ’\n    86вҶ’**Old plan**: Single 3-state HMM\n    87вҶ’**New plan**: 4-layer hierarchy\n    88вҶ’\n    89вҶ’| Layer | Method | Update Frequency | Purpose |\n    90вҶ’|-------|--------|-----------------|---------|\n    91вҶ’| Fast (every bar) | Efficiency Ratio + GARCH vol | O(1) | Quick regime estimate |\n    92вҶ’| Core (every bar) | 2-state HMM (filtered probs) + BOCPD | O(KВІ) | State identification + change detection |\n    93вҶ’| Slow (hourly) | Rolling Hurst (24h DFA) | O(window) | Trending vs mean-reverting context |\n    94вҶ’| Meta (weekly refit) | LightGBM on all above | Batch | Optimal regime label |\n    95вҶ’\n    96вҶ’**Why**: BOCPD detects changes 2-10 bars faster than HMM alone. Efficiency Ratio is the highest signal-to-complexity feature for trend vs range. Hurst provides macro context.\n    97вҶ’\n    98вҶ’### 5. Event-Driven Macro Module (Highest Single Edge)\n    99вҶ’\n   100вҶ’**New finding**: NQ reaction to macro events (CPI, FOMC) leads BTC by 2-5 minutes with ~62-68% accuracy."}]},"uuid":"41cfa4c4-430b-45e0-a02f-91f9a8816595","timestamp":"2026-03-23T13:33:47.075Z","sourceToolAssistantUUID":"875937f1-33b1-49d9-9963-3c94f26f9b16","userType":"external","entrypoint":"claude-vscode","cwd":"/Users/edgarpocaterra/ep2-crypto","sessionId":"f48c9af0-2e30-4c92-9024-4c84a03f39db","version":"2.1.81","gitBranch":"main","slug":"spicy-gathering-plum"}

It was a structural break.\n   233вҶ’\n   234вҶ’**Setup code:**\n   235вҶ’\n   236вҶ’```python\n   237вҶ’class TestFTXCollapse:\n   238вҶ’    \"\"\"Replay November 6-11, 2022 through the full system.\"\"\"\n   239вҶ’\n   240вҶ’    @pytest.fixture\n   241вҶ’    def scenario_data(self):\n   242вҶ’        return load_historical_scenario(\n   243вҶ’            start=datetime(2022, 11, 4, tzinfo=timezone.utc),\n   244вҶ’            end=datetime(2022, 11, 13, tzinfo=timezone.utc),\n   245вҶ’            symbol=\"BTC/USDT:USDT\",\n   246вҶ’            include_orderbook=True,\n   247вҶ’            include_liquidations=True,\n   248вҶ’            include_funding=True,\n   249вҶ’            spread_multiplier=3.0,\n   250вҶ’            depth_multiplier=0.5,\n   251вҶ’            slippage_multiplier=2.5,\n   252вҶ’            # FTX-specific: negative funding, exchange-driven selling\n   253вҶ’            pre_crash_funding_rate=-0.03,\n   254вҶ’        )\n   255вҶ’\n   256вҶ’    def test_regime_detector_flags_anomaly(self, scenario_data):\n   257вҶ’        \"\"\"Regime detector should flag this as an unseen regime or\n   258вҶ’        high transition probability (instability).\"\"\"\n   259вҶ’        result = self._run_backtest(scenario_data)\n   260вҶ’        # BOCPD change point detection should fire\n   261вҶ’        assert result.regime_change_points > 0\n   262вҶ’        # Regime uncertainty should be elevated\n   263вҶ’        max_regime_entropy = max(result.regime_entropy_series)\n   264вҶ’        assert max_regime_entropy > 0.8, (\n   265вҶ’            f\"Regime entropy peaked at {max_regime_entropy:.2f}, \"\n   266вҶ’            \"expected > 0.8 during structural break\"\n   267вҶ’        )\n   268вҶ’\n   269вҶ’    def test_slow_bleed_detection(self, scenario_data):\n   270вҶ’        \"\"\"System must handle slow multi-day drawdown, not just flash crashes.\"\"\"\n   271вҶ’        result = self._run_backtest(scenario_data)\n   272вҶ’        # Weekly loss limit (5%) should trigger\n   273вҶ’        assert result.weekly_loss_limit_triggered is True\n   274вҶ’\n   275вҶ’    def test_no_buy_the_dip_during_crisis(self, scenario_data):\n   276вҶ’        \"\"\"Model should not aggressively go long during a confidence crisis.\"\"\"\n   277вҶ’        result = self._run_backtest(scenario_data)\n   278вҶ’        long_trades_during_crisis = [\n   279вҶ’            t for t in result.trades\n   280вҶ’            if t.direction == \"long\"\n   281вҶ’            and t.timestamp >= datetime(2022, 11, 8, tzinfo=timezone.utc)\n   282вҶ’            and t.timestamp <= datetime(2022, 11, 11, tzinfo=timezone.utc)\n   283вҶ’        ]\n   284вҶ’        # Some long trades are acceptable, but net direction should be flat/short\n   285вҶ’        assert len(long_trades_during_crisis) < 5, (\n   286вҶ’            f\"{len(long_trades_during_crisis)} long trades during FTX crisis\"\n   287вҶ’        )\n   288вҶ’```\n   289вҶ’\n   290вҶ’**Pass/fail criteria:**\n   291вҶ’| Criterion | Pass | Fail |\n   292вҶ’|-----------|------|------|\n   293вҶ’| Regime anomaly detected | BOCPD fires, entropy > 0.8 | No change point detected |\n   294вҶ’| Weekly loss limit | Triggered | Not triggered after 5 days of losses |\n   295вҶ’| Long trades during crisis | < 5 | >= 5 (model buying the dip blindly) |\n   296вҶ’| Max drawdown | < 15% | >= 15% |\n   297вҶ’\n   298вҶ’**Hardening if test fails:**\n   299вҶ’- If regime detector misses the structural break: Add a \"correlation breakdown\" feature -- when the rolling BTC-NQ correlation drops by >0.3 in 24 hours, flag as regime anomaly.\n   300вҶ’- If model keeps going long: Add an exchange health check to the confidence gating pipeline. If exchange withdrawal suspensions are detected (monitor via API status endpoints), reduce confidence by 50%.\n   301вҶ’\n   302вҶ’---\n   303вҶ’\n   304вҶ’### 1.4 March 2023 SVB Banking Crisis (BTC +20% on USDC depeg)\n   305вҶ’\n   306вҶ’**What happened (March 10-13, 2023):**\n   307вҶ’- Silicon Valley Bank collapsed on March 10. USDC (backed partly by SVB deposits) depegged to ~$0.87.\n   308вҶ’- BTC/USD initially dropped ~5% on contagion fear, then rallied ~20% over the next 3 days as crypto was viewed as an alternative to the banking system.\n   309вҶ’- USDC-quoted pairs showed artificial BTC price inflation (BTC/USDC spiked because USDC was worth less, not because BTC was worth more in real terms).\n   310вҶ’- Funding rates spiked positive as longs piled in during the \"digital gold\" narrative.\n   311вҶ’- Cross-market: S&P 500/NQ dropped on banking fears, but BTC moved in the OPPOSITE direction -- a rare and significant decorrelation event.\n   312вҶ’- This was a regime where the BTC-NQ correlation flipped from positive to negative overnight.\n   313вҶ’\n   314вҶ’**Setup code:**\n   315вҶ’\n   316вҶ’```python\n   317вҶ’class TestSVBCrisis:\n   318вҶ’    \"\"\"Replay March 10-13, 2023 through the full system.\"\"\"\n   319вҶ’\n   320вҶ’    @pytest.fixture\n   321вҶ’    def scenario_data(self):\n   322вҶ’        return load_historical_scenario(\n   323вҶ’            start=datetime(2023, 3, 9, tzinfo=timezone.utc),\n   324вҶ’            end=datetime(2023, 3, 15, tzinfo=timezone.utc),\n   325вҶ’            symbol=\"BTC/USDT:USDT\",\n   326вҶ’            include_orderbook=True,\n   327вҶ’            include_funding=True,\n   328вҶ’            # USDC depeg creates data anomalies\n   329вҶ’            stablecoin_depeg=True,\n   330вҶ’            spread_multiplier=4.0,\n   331вҶ’            depth_multiplier=0.4,\n   332вҶ’        )\n   333вҶ’\n   334вҶ’    def test_stablecoin_depeg_handling(self, scenario_data):\n   335вҶ’        \"\"\"System must not confuse USDC depeg with real BTC price movement.\n   336вҶ’        If using USDT-quoted pairs, impact should be minimal, but cross-exchange\n   337вҶ’        basis divergence should trigger a warning.\"\"\"\n   338вҶ’        result = self._run_backtest(scenario_data)\n   339вҶ’        assert result.data_quality_warnings.get(\"basis_divergence\") is True\n   340вҶ’\n   341вҶ’    def test_decorrelation_detected(self, scenario_data):\n   342вҶ’        \"\"\"BTC-NQ correlation flipped from ~0.6 to negative.\n   343вҶ’        System must detect and adapt.\"\"\"\n   344вҶ’        result = self._run_backtest(scenario_data)\n   345вҶ’        # Tests graceful re-entry logic.\n   525вҶ’\n   526вҶ’**Setup code:**\n   527вҶ’\n   528вҶ’```python\n   529вҶ’class TestRepeatedFlashCrashes:\n   530вҶ’    \"\"\"10 flash crashes of -5% to -10% each, spaced 12-24 hours apart.\"\"\"\n   531вҶ’\n   532вҶ’    @pytest.fixture\n   533вҶ’    def scenario_data(self):\n   534вҶ’        builder = SyntheticScenarioBuilder(\n   535вҶ’            base_price=50000.0,\n   536вҶ’            duration_hours=168,  # 1 week\n   537вҶ’            bar_interval_minutes=5,\n   538вҶ’        )\n   539вҶ’        # Normal volatility with 10 injected crash events\n   540вҶ’        builder.set_price_path(volatility_annualized=60.0)\n   541вҶ’        crash_times_hours = [8, 22, 38, 55, 72, 88, 104, 118, 135, 155]\n   542вҶ’        for t in crash_times_hours:\n   543вҶ’            builder.inject_crash(\n   544вҶ’                time_offset_hours=t,\n   545вҶ’                magnitude_pct=np.random.uniform(-10, -5),\n   546вҶ’                duration_minutes=np.random.randint(5, 30),\n   547вҶ’                recovery_pct=np.random.uniform(0.3, 0.7),\n   548вҶ’                recovery_minutes=np.random.randint(30, 120),\n   549вҶ’            )\n   550вҶ’        builder.set_orderbook(\n   551вҶ’            spread_bps=1.0,\n   552вҶ’            depth_normal=True,\n   553вҶ’            crash_spread_multiplier=8.0,\n   554вҶ’            crash_depth_multiplier=0.2,\n   555вҶ’        )\n   556вҶ’        return builder.build()\n   557вҶ’\n   558вҶ’    def test_weekly_loss_limit_triggers(self, scenario_data):\n   559вҶ’        \"\"\"Weekly loss limit (5%) must trigger and halt trading.\"\"\"\n   560вҶ’        result = self._run_backtest(scenario_data)\n   561вҶ’        assert result.weekly_loss_limit_triggered is True\n   562вҶ’\n   563вҶ’    def test_kill_switch_recovery(self, scenario_data):\n   564вҶ’        \"\"\"After kill switch triggers, system must recover trading\n   565вҶ’        after the defined cooldown period.\"\"\"\n   566вҶ’        result = self._run_backtest(scenario_data)\n   567вҶ’        # Should have at least 2 kill switch activations (daily or weekly)\n   568вҶ’        assert result.kill_switch_activations >= 2\n   569вҶ’        # Should also have at least 1 recovery (resumed trading)\n   570вҶ’        assert result.kill_switch_recoveries >= 1\n   571вҶ’\n   572вҶ’    def test_drawdown_gate_graduated_reentry(self, scenario_data):\n   573вҶ’        \"\"\"After drawdown, position sizes should gradually increase,\n   574вҶ’        not snap back to full size.\"\"\"\n   575вҶ’        result = self._run_backtest(scenario_data)\n   576вҶ’        # Find position sizes after first recovery\n   577вҶ’        recovery_sizes = result.post_recovery_position_sizes\n   578вҶ’        if len(recovery_sizes) >= 3:\n   579вҶ’            # First recovery trade should be small\n   580вҶ’            assert recovery_sizes[0] < 3.0  # < 3% vs normal 4-5%\n   581вҶ’            # Should gradually increase\n   582вҶ’            assert recovery_sizes[-1] > recovery_sizes[0]\n   583вҶ’\n   584вҶ’    def test_cumulative_drawdown_bounded(self, scenario_data):\n   585вҶ’        \"\"\"Even with 10 crashes, cumulative drawdown must be bounded.\"\"\"\n   586вҶ’        result = self._run_backtest(scenario_data)\n   587вҶ’        assert result.max_drawdown_pct < 20.0, (\n   588вҶ’            f\"Cumulative drawdown {result.max_drawdown_pct:.1f}% exceeded \"\n   589вҶ’            \"20% across 10 flash crashes\"\n   590вҶ’        )\n   591вҶ’```\n   592вҶ’\n   593вҶ’**Pass/fail criteria:**\n   594вҶ’| Criterion | Pass | Fail |\n   595вҶ’|-----------|------|------|\n   596вҶ’| Weekly loss limit | Triggered | Not triggered |\n   597вҶ’| Kill switch recovery | >= 1 recovery | No recovery (system stuck) |\n   598вҶ’| Graduated re-entry | First post-recovery trade < 3% | Full size immediately |\n   599вҶ’| Cumulative drawdown | < 20% | >= 20% |\n   600вҶ’\n   601вҶ’---\n   602вҶ’\n   603вҶ’### 2.3 Exchange Suspends Withdrawals (Confidence Crisis)\n   604вҶ’\n   605вҶ’**What this tests:** A scenario where the exchange we trade on (Binance) announces withdrawal suspension. This is an FTX-like event where the correct action is to close all positions and wait.\n   606вҶ’\n   607вҶ’```python\n   608вҶ’class TestExchangeWithdrawalSuspension:\n   609вҶ’    \"\"\"Simulate exchange withdrawal suspension mid-trade.\"\"\"\n   610вҶ’\n   611вҶ’    @pytest.fixture\n   612вҶ’    def scenario_data(self):\n   613вҶ’        builder = SyntheticScenarioBuilder(\n   614вҶ’            base_price=50000.0,\n   615вҶ’            duration_hours=72,\n   616вҶ’            bar_interval_minutes=5,\n   617вҶ’        )\n   618вҶ’        builder.set_price_path(volatility_annualized=80.0)\n   619вҶ’        # At T+24h, inject withdrawal suspension event\n   620вҶ’        builder.inject_event(\n   621вҶ’            time_offset_hours=24,\n   622вҶ’            event_type=\"withdrawal_suspension\",\n   623вҶ’            # Price drops -15% over 4 hours after announcement\n   624вҶ’            price_impact_pct=-15.0,\n   625вҶ’            impact_duration_hours=4,\n   626вҶ’            # Volume spikes 5x\n   627вҶ’            volume_multiplier=5.0,\n   628вҶ’            # Spread widens 10x\n   629вҶ’            spread_multiplier=10.0,\n   630вҶ’        )\n   631вҶ’        return builder.build()\n   632вҶ’\n   633вҶ’    def test_emergency_close_on_suspension(self, scenario_data):\n   634вҶ’        \"\"\"If system has an open position when withdrawal suspension\n   635вҶ’        is detected, it must close immediately regardless of PnL.\"\"\"\n   636вҶ’        result = self._run_backtest(scenario_data)\n   637вҶ’        open_positions_after_event = [\n   638вҶ’            p for p in result.position_log\n   639вҶ’            if p.is_open\n   640вҶ’            and p.timestamp > scenario_data.event_timestamp\n   641вҶ’        ]\n   642вҶ’        # All positions should be closed within 5 minutes of event\n   643вҶ’        for pos in open_positions_after_event:\n   644вҶ’            time_to_close = (\n   645вҶ’                pos.close_timestamp - scenario_data.event_timestamp\n   646вҶ’            ).total_seconds()\n   647вҶ’            assert time_to_close < 300, (\n   648вҶ’                f\"Position still open {time_to_close:.0f}s after \"\n   649вҶ’                \"withdrawal suspension\"\n   650вҶ’            )\n   651вҶ’\n   652вҶ’    def test_no_new_trades_after_suspension(self, scenario_data):\n   653вҶ’        \"\"\"No new positions should be opened after withdrawal suspension.\"\"\"\n   654вҶ’        result = self._run_backtest(scenario_data)\n   655вҶ’        post_event_entries = [\n   656вҶ’            t for t in result.trades\n   657вҶ’            if t.entry_timestamp > scenario_data.event_timestamp\n   658вҶ’        ]\n   659вҶ’        assert len(post_event_entries) == 0\n   660вҶ’```\n   661вҶ’\n   662вҶ’---\n   663вҶ’\n   664вҶ’### 2.4 Regulatory Ban Announcement (Step-Change Regime Shift)\n   665вҶ’\n   666вҶ’**What this tests:** A permanent regime shift where the old model is suddenly invalid.
